### Compression

- `P1.1`

- `P1.10`
  Equation:

## Direct Operational Meaning

A bathed-and-labeled program: first prove stability, then run the long convergence ladder, then name the stable nodes so the whole network can be replayed as a system. Process statistics: 86 circulation commands (qo-); 14 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 13 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 8 completion markers (daiin).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f82r` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=86, N_valve=14, and N_seal=2. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f82r` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.
